	focus = {
		id = ENG_the_prince_trust
		icon = ENG_charles_2000

		x = -5
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = ENG_the_queens_family
		text_icon = GER_inner_circle_focus_style
		cost = 2

		prerequisite = {
			focus = ENG_the_queens_family
		}

		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				hidden_trigger = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_charles_was_ascended_flag } #Flag to prevent AI from taking the focus again after advisor has been replaced}
				}
			}

			has_country_flag = ENG_elisabeth_ruling_monarch
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ENG_inner_circle_event_pending_flag
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_inner_circle_event_pending_flag }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ENG_inner_circle_event_pending_flag
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_inner_circle_event_pending_flag }
			}

			ENG_inner_circle_is_ascension_cd_over = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ENG_inner_circle_cd_flag
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = ENG_inner_circle_cd_days_tt
					NOT = {	has_country_flag = ENG_inner_circle_cd_flag }
				}
			}
		}

		#Focus will need to pause while events are pending
		cancel_if_invalid = no
		continue_if_invalid = no

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INNER_CIRCLE  FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		select_effect = { #Necessary to prevent AI from getting stuck if the focus is paused due to available trigger returning false
			set_country_flag = ENG_charles_ascension_flag
		}

		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = ENG_ascension_of_character_tt
				CHARACTER = ENG_prince_charles
			}
			show_ideas_tooltip = ENG_charles_1_idea
			newline = yes

			unlock_decision_tooltip = {
				decision = ENG_charles_charities_network_decision
				show_effect_tooltip = yes
				show_modifiers = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = ENG_charles_charities_network_decision_activated

			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt

			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = ENG_ascension_of_character_focus_tt
				CHARACTER = ENG_prince_charles
			}

			if = { #Just to make it easy to debug stuff for development
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_1 = 1 }
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_2 = 1 }
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_3 = 1 }
					}
				}
				log = "Advisor was already there. STOP CHEATING!"
			}
			else_if = { # ASCENDED ADVISORS FULL - NEED TO REPLACE SOMEONE
				limit = {
					check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_1 = 0 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_2 = 0 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_3 = 0 compare = not_equals }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { ENG_ascending_advisor = 1 }
					country_event = ENG_inner_circle.01
					country_event ={
						id = ENG_inner_circle_charles.07
						days = 50
						random_days = 25
					}
				}

				custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt
				custom_effect_tooltip = {
					localization_key = ENG_event_to_replace_ascended_advisor_tt
					EVENT = ENG_inner_circle.01.t
					CHARACTER = ENG_prince_charles
				}
			}
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ideas = ENG_charles_1_idea
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_1 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_1 = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_2 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_2 = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_3 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_3 = 1 }
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ENG_inner_circle_charles.01 days = ENG_inner_circle_days_to_start_focus random_days = ENG_inner_circle_random_days }

				clr_country_flag = ENG_charles_ascension_flag

				ENG_inner_circle_set_ascension_cd = yes

				if = { #If historical make sure Todt is not picked ever after being replaced by Speer in the Intrigue Event
					limit = {
						GER_is_historical_ai = yes
					}
					set_country_flag = ENG_charles_was_ascended_flag #Flag to prevent AI from taking the focus again after advisor has been replaced
				}
				else = {
					set_country_flag = { #Flag to prevent AI from taking the focus again after advisor has been replaced
						flag = ENG_charles_was_ascended_flag
						days = 1500 # Clear after ~4 years
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				CHARACTER = ENG_prince_andrew
			}

						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_1 = 2 }

						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_3 = 2 }
					}
				}
				log = "Advisor was already there. STOP CHEATING!"
			}
			else_if = { # ASCENDED ADVISORS FULL - NEED TO REPLACE SOMEONE
				limit = {
					check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_1 = 0 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_2 = 0 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_3 = 0 compare = not_equals }
				}
				hidden_effect = {

					CHARACTER = ENG_prince_andrew
				}
			}

					add_ideas = ENG_andrew_1_idea
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_1 = 0 }
					}

						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_3 = 0 }

				}
			}

					}

				}
				else = {

				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ENG_inner_circle_event_pending_flag
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_inner_circle_event_pending_flag }
			}

			ENG_inner_circle_is_ascension_cd_over = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ENG_inner_circle_cd_flag
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = ENG_inner_circle_cd_days_tt
					NOT = {	has_country_flag = ENG_inner_circle_cd_flag }
				}
			}
		}

		#Focus will need to pause while events are pending
		cancel_if_invalid = no

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INNER_CIRCLE FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		select_effect = { #Necessary to prevent AI from getting stuck if the focus is paused due to available trigger returning false
			set_country_flag = ENG_philip_ascension_flag
		}

		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = ENG_ascension_of_character_tt
				CHARACTER = ENG_prince_phillip
			}
			show_ideas_tooltip = ENG_phillip_1_idea

			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt
			unlock_decision_tooltip = {
				decision = ENG_philip_trust_funds_grants_decision
				show_effect_tooltip = yes
				show_modifiers = yes
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = ENG_ascension_of_character_focus_tt
				CHARACTER = ENG_prince_phillip
			}

			if = { #Just to make it easy to debug stuff for development
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_1 = 5 }
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_2 = 5 }
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_3 = 5 }
					}
				}
				log = "Advisor was already there. STOP CHEATING!"
			}
			else_if = { # ASCENDED ADVISORS FULL - NEED TO REPLACE SOMEONE
				limit = {
					check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_1 = 0 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_2 = 0 compare = not_equals }
					check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_3 = 0 compare = not_equals }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { ENG_ascending_advisor = 5 }
					country_event = ENG_inner_circle.01
				}

				custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt
				custom_effect_tooltip = {
					localization_key = ENG_event_to_replace_ascended_advisor_tt
					EVENT = ENG_inner_circle.01.t
					CHARACTER = ENG_prince_phillip
				}
			}
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ideas = ENG_phillip_1_idea
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_1 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_1 = 5 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_2 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_2 = 5 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_3 = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { ENG_ascended_advisor_3 = 5 }
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ENG_inner_circle_philip.01 days = ENG_inner_circle_days_to_start_focus random_days = ENG_inner_circle_random_days }

				clr_country_flag = ENG_philip_ascension_flag

				ENG_inner_circle_set_ascension_cd = yes

				if = { #If historical make sure Todt is not picked ever after being replaced by Speer in the Intrigue Event
					limit = {
						ENG_is_historical_ai = yes
					}
					set_country_flag = ENG_philip_was_ascended_flag #Flag to prevent AI from taking the focus again after advisor has been replaced
				}
				else = {
					set_country_flag = { #Flag to prevent AI from taking the focus again after advisor has been replaced
						flag = ENG_philip_was_ascended_flag
						days = 1500 # Clear after ~4 years
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
